           <div class="module has-bottom-divider">
            <section class="media-item ">
             <div class="media-item__summary size--large">
              <header class="summary-header">
               <p class="category">
                <a class="js-tealium-tracking" data-tracking="mpos=center&amp;mid=b_top_hero&amp;lindex=1&amp;lcol=item_solo" href="https://www.politico.com/magazine/tag/white-house" target="_top">
                 White House
                </a>
               </p>
              </header>
              <h3 class="headline ">
               <a class="js-tealium-tracking" data-tracking="mpos=center&amp;mid=b_top_hero&amp;lindex=1&amp;lcol=item_solo" href="https://www.politico.com/news/2021/03/02/neera-tanden-biden-withdraw-472980" target="_top">
                Neera Tanden withdraws as Biden’s budget chief pick
               </a>
              </h3>
              <p class="dek">
               The president’s statement indicated he expects Tanden to serve in another role in his administration.
              </p>
              <div class="meta">
               <div class="meta__details">
                <p class="authors">
                 By
                 <span class="vcard">

             <header class="summary-header">

              </p>

             <h1 class="headline" data-tracking-text="The U.S. Has the Power to Tamp Down Coronavirus Variants — If We’re Willing to Use It">
              The U.S. Has the Power to Tamp Down Coronavirus Variants — If We’re Willing to Use It
             </h1>
             <p class="dek">
              We’re in a race against mutations all around the world. The fastest way to speed vaccination is to let other countries manufacture the vaccines developed by Operation Warp Speed.
             </p>
             <div class="meta">
              <div class="meta__details">
               <p class="authors">
                By
                <span class="vcard">
                 Tom Frieden
                </span>
                and
                <span class="vcard">
                 Marine Buissonnière
                </span>
               </p>
              </div>
             </div>

          <a aria-label="How Biden Is Setting Himself Apart From Trump—and Obama—in the Middle East" class="slider__card js-tealium-tracking" data-tracking="mpos=center&amp;mid=d_full_width&amp;lindex=3&amp;lcol=mag_slider" href="https://www.politico.com/news/magazine/2021/03/02/how-biden-is-setting-himself-apart-from-trumpand-obamain-the-middle-east-472413" target="_top">
           <section class="media-item is-magazine">
            <div class="media-item__image">
             <div class="media-item__image-wrapper">
              <img alt="U.S. President Joe Biden speaks at an event to sign an Executive Order on the economy with Vice President Kamala Harris February 24, 2021 in the State Dining Room of the White House in Washington, DC." data-lazy="https://static.politico.com/dims4/default/020d28d/2147483647/resize/424x/quality/90/?url=https%3A%2F%2Fstatic.politico.com%2Fa2%2F9f%2Fdbd13dbf48b6829c8d73f36b590f%2Fgettyimages-1303924941-1-1.jpg" size="feature-carousel" src="/images/website/shared/template/trans-3by2-placeholder.png" title="U.S. President Joe Biden speaks at an event to sign an Executive Order on the economy with Vice President Kamala Harris February 24, 2021 in the State Dining Room of the White House in Washington, DC."/>

            <div class="media-item__summary is-centered">
             <header class="summary-header">
              <p class="category">
               OPINION |
Washington and the World
              </p>
             </header>
             <h1 class="headline" data-tracking-text="How Biden Is Setting Himself Apart From Trump—and Obama—in the Middle East">
              How Biden Is Setting Himself Apart From Trump—and Obama—in the Middle East
             </h1>
             <p class="dek">
              The new president is trying to uphold American values while acknowledging cold realities. But the balance will be difficult to maintain.
             </p>
             <div class="meta">
              <div class="meta__details">
               <p class="authors">
